The Special Party Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, in conjunction with the Railway Administration and the trade unions of the two railways, decided that all employees and cleaners of the entire railway would donate one day's salary. They had already remitted 20,000 yuan on the 18th of last month to comfort the soldiers at the front. The Special Party Department of the railway has also dispatched staff to guide the teachers and students of the Rotary elementary schools along the two railways to donate funds for comfort. All teachers and staff of the nine Rotary elementary schools in Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Suzhou, Shanghai, Wusong, Zhabei, Ningbo, and Baisha donated one day's salary, and students saved one corner, two corners, or three corners of candy and snack money each. Workers also voluntarily donated one day's salary. Senior students from each school also organized donation teams to solicit donations at various stations. The teachers and students of each school worked very hard. As of yesterday, the Wusong Rotary Elementary School had donated the most items, totaling 276.17 yuan in national currency. The school's principal, Tang Jianzhou, teacher representative Xu Ying, and student representatives Tang Lusheng, Wang Yanqing, Shen Chengzhu, and Li Xinyi, personally brought the donations to the Special Party Department of the two railways for verification and collection. The Nanjing Rotary Elementary School donated 86.46 yuan in national currency, the Zhabei Rotary Elementary School donated 47.90 yuan in national currency, and another 2.40 yuan in national currency, 10 jiao in silver dollars, and 646 copper coins. The Zhenjiang Rotary Elementary School donated 28.83 yuan in national currency, and another 8 jiao in silver dollars and 506 copper coins. The Baisha Rotary Elementary School donated 14 yuan in national currency. All of these donations have been remitted to the Special Party Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, which will forward them to the Central Finance Committee for distribution to the soldiers at the front.

Sincere Employees

All employees of the Sincere Company and its affiliated businesses initiated a salary donation day, totaling 1,005.98 yuan in national currency. Yesterday, they entrusted the Bank of China to remit the money to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan to be distributed to the soldiers at the front.

Rickshaw Pullers on Two Railways

The rickshaw pullers on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways voluntarily initiated a donation to aid Suiyuan. All 260-plus people saved on food and clothing and collected 102.10 yuan in national currency, which has been submitted to the Railway Administration for remittance.

China Advertising Firm

All employees of the China Advertising Company and its affiliated Shida Printing Company on Hong Kong Road promoted a one-day movement to help Suiyuan, totaling 190 yuan in French currency, which was handed over to this newspaper for remittance to the front.

Liyuan Farm

All employees submitted 8.80 yuan for the Suiyuan soldiers' comfort fund, entrusting this newspaper to remit it to the front.

Coal Industry Association

Initiated a fundraising campaign, raising 900 yuan, which has been handed over to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for remittance to the soldiers at the front in Suiyuan.

Samsung Cotton and Iron Factory

Colleagues donated 60.08 yuan in French currency, which was handed over to this newspaper for remittance to the front.

Italian Embassy in China Denies Recognizing Manchukuo, States that the Consulate in Shenyang is Merely Being Reopened, an Administrative Measure That Cannot Be Seen as Recognition —Lojacono Explains to the Press in Geneva— 94

According to the *Xin Sheng She*, Italy and Japan have formally announced the establishment of the agreement between the two parties in a public statement. However, regarding the exchange of recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia and Manchukuo, it only mentioned that Japan would close its embassy in Abyssinia and establish a consulate in Addis Ababa, avoiding mentioning Italy's establishment of a consulate in Shenyang and instead issuing a written statement. Yesterday, a reporter from *Xin Sheng She* inquired again at the Italian Embassy in Shanghai about everything. Mr. Ross, the Chinese Secretary, came out to meet him. Mr. Ross still denied that Italy had recognized Manchukuo, saying that the Italian government would definitely not formally recognize Manchukuo. Italy had originally established a consulate in Shenyang, which was later closed. This time, it is only planned to be reopened, not newly established. This is a change in administrative measures and cannot be immediately regarded as recognition of Manchukuo. So far, no government statement has been received here. Regarding this matter, Ambassador Lojacono will hold a press conference in Geneva within days to explain it in detail.

Hangzhou-Yushan Section Replaced with Heavy Rails, Loan Agreement Signed, Amount of 2.8 Million Chinese Yuan, Three Banks Underwrite the Loan, Formal Contract to be Signed After Council Approval 96

The Hangzhou-Yushan section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway (formerly the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway) has decided to replace its rails with 63-pound heavy rails so that it can operate heavy cars like the Yushan-Nanchang and Nanchang-Pingxiang sections. It is in the process of borrowing 2.8 million yuan from the Shanghai syndicate of China Bank, Agricultural Bank of China, and Zhejiang Local Bank for the rail replacement project. After negotiations between the syndicate representative Jin Runquan, the manager of the Hangzhou branch of the Bank of China, and the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau in Hangzhou, and after consulting with Shanghai, a reporter from the *Xin Xin She* learned from the syndicate that the draft loan contract had been negotiated in Hangzhou and approved by the syndicate. The draft was signed first on the morning of the 2nd at the Hangzhou branch of the Bank of China, with the Bank of China agreeing to lend 1.8 million yuan and the Agricultural Bank of China and Zhejiang Local Bank each agreeing to lend 500,000 yuan, to be repaid in six years with an annual interest rate of 1%. The formal contract will be signed after the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau submits it for approval at the council meeting on the 8th.

Chief Director Gong Xianzhou presided over the meeting, and the timing and route of the coffin's removal were decided and personnel were assigned to make arrangements. The meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM.

Order of Funeral Service

The order of the funeral service has been arranged: (1) At 10:00 AM on the 5th, a family memorial service will be held, followed by the sons in mourning attire acting as masters of ceremonies. In the afternoon, relatives will pay their respects. (2) Before 10:00 AM on the 6th, all members of the funeral committee will hold a public memorial service. From 11:00 AM to 12:30 PM, ambassadors and ministers from various countries in China and consuls in Shanghai will pay their respects. Representatives from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai office and the municipal government will be responsible for the reception. In the afternoon, officials from various party, government, and military agencies in Shanghai and representatives from various sectors will pay their respects. (3) At 12:00 noon on the 7th, the coffin will be moved for burial.

Burial Route

Before the coffin is transported to the North Railway Station, the route will be from Avenue Joffre, via Avenue Petain, Rue Yu Ya Ching, Peking Road, turning into Chekiang Road, North Chekiang Road, Boundary Road, and reaching the North Railway Station. Memorial sheds will be set up along the route, including at Eight Immortals Bridge, the intersection of Rue Yu Ya Ching and Nanking Road, the intersection of Peking Road and Chekiang Road, and the North Railway Station.

Procession

The procession for the funeral will include: (1) 16 mounted police officers (police station), (2) a military band (Public Security Bureau), (3) a memorial banner pavilion, (4) a platoon of honor guards (security team), (5) a photo pavilion, (6) 240 monks and Taoists, (7) a military band (Garrison Command), (8) a spirit tablet sedan chair honor guard (military police), (9) guests attending the funeral, (10) pallbearers, (11) a group of mourning sons, (12) the hearse, (13) the bereaved family. The funeral committee has requested Inspector General Da Zhui of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Section Chief Li Dachao of the First Section of the Municipal Government, and Secretary Wang Zhinan of the Songhu Garrison Command to serve as the chief and deputy commanders of the procession.

Hearse Itinerary

The train carrying the hearse consists of 18 cars, originally specially built for the death of Empress Dowager Cixi of the Qing Dynasty, and has been in the custody of the Beining Railway. The train has now arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin. The special train for transporting the coffin is scheduled to depart from the North Station at 5:00 PM on the 7th, arrive at Kunshan at 6:08 PM, depart at 6:30 PM, arrive at Suzhou at 7:30 PM, depart at 8:00 PM, arrive at Wuxi at 9:05 PM, depart at 9:25 PM, arrive at Changzhou at 10:15 PM, depart at 10:46 PM, arrive at Danyang at 11:49 PM, depart at 12:12 AM on the 8th, arrive at Zhenjiang at 12:55 AM, depart at 1:30 AM, arrive at Yaohuamen at 3:05 AM, depart at 7:30 AM, and arrive at Nanjing at 8:00 AM. After various public memorial services in Beijing, it will cross the river and is scheduled to depart from Pukou North at 2:00 PM on the 8th, arrive at Xuzhou at 12:00 PM, arrive at Jinan at 9:00 AM on the 9th, arrive at Tianjin at 6:00 PM, and arrive at Qianmen in Beiping at 8:00 AM on the 10th. The coffin will then be moved directly from Qianmen to the Temple of the Reclining Buddha in the Western Hills for burial.

Article 12: All committee members of the association are volunteers, and association staff may be given travel expenses at discretion. (5) Supplementary Provisions: Article 13: The detailed rules for the various committees of the association will be determined separately. Article 14: These articles of association shall be implemented upon adoption by the association.

Public Security Bureau's Special One-Month Exhibition for Smokers to Exchange Licenses; More than 40,000 Received Licenses in the Previous Period; Smoking Without Exchange After Deadline Will Be Prosecuted 105

The anti-drug affairs of this city are the responsibility of the Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee, the Public Security Bureau, and other agencies. The procedures for smokers to obtain licenses have been handled by the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Public Security Branch Bureaus and Teams, which have achieved considerable results. More than 40,000 people received smoker licenses in the second period. The period for exchanging the third period smoke licenses began on the 1st of last month and was originally scheduled to end at the end of last month. Later, because more than 30,000 smokers went to exchange their smoke licenses within the deadline, some smokers did not have time to exchange them. The authorities specially considered this and extended the deadline for another month, until the end of this month. No further extensions will be granted, and old licenses will be invalidated if they are not exchanged after the deadline, and they will be prosecuted for private smoking. The Municipal Public Security Bureau has issued a public notice to inform the smokers of this city in order to avoid them committing crimes due to exceeding the deadline, which would lead to regret.

The Price of Sha Tian (Sand Field) is Still Allowed to be Collected at Half Price, Limited to Before January of Next Year; Absolutely No Further Extension After That 107

The Third Shatin Branch Bureau of Jiangsu Province, in view of the fact that some of the fields released before May 1929 that have not been enclosed still have unpaid field prices, although the deadline for collecting half price has been extended repeatedly, it is still not common. The bureau, in view of this, re-submitted a request to the Jiangsu Finance Department to allow half-price collection. After receiving the submission, the Finance Department has approved it. All fields released before May 1929 that have not been enclosed and for which the field price is paid before January 20, 1937, will still be allowed to collect at half price. No further extensions will be granted after that.

Joint Meeting of the Lawyers Association's Executive and Supervisory Committees 110

The Shanghai Lawyers Association convened its 26th executive committee meeting at 7:00 PM the day before yesterday at the association's office at No. 30 Avenue de Corneille in the French Concession. Qin Liankui was elected as chairman, Dai Jixian recorded, and the meeting was opened as scheduled. Record of motions: (A) Report matters: (omitted) (B) Discussion matters: (1) How should this association promote the Shanghai Municipal National Contribution One-Day Income Movement? Resolved: Lawyers do not necessarily have income every day, so it is difficult to apply the one-day income method. Members can only donate freely, but the one-day income movement is still promoted. (2) The Judicial Administration Department has approved the request to amend Section 7 of the Measures for Lawyers Performing Duties in County Judicial Offices, regarding criminal cases, such as when the county magistrate appears in court, the lawyer can naturally appear in court to perform his duties, and does not prohibit lawyers from appearing in court at all. Resolved: The reply will be attached with opinions and forwarded to the Lawyers Association of the Republic of China for handling. (3) The Shanghai District Court Prosecutor has issued an order to rectify the lawyers' discipline, formulate measures, and order compliance, and forward it to all members for compliance. Resolved: Notify all members. (4) The Shanghai District Court Prosecutor has issued an order that meetings should be reported in advance in the future. Resolved: Handle in accordance with the regulations. This association has no such obligation if there is no provision in the charter. (5) Member Li Aokui proposed that the banditry on the border is causing national outrage, and we should initiate the purchase of gas masks and transport them to the front lines. Resolved: This type of organization has already been established in this city, so there is no need to initiate it. If members have donations, they can contact the organization directly. (6) Standing Committee Member Shen Junru applied to resign from the position of Standing Committee Member. Resolved: Unanimously retained. (7) Xu Zuoliang proposed that the association and various newspapers should specifically designate a special column for the association members' announcements in newspapers, and limit the length to maintain discipline. Resolved: Chen Tingrui and Zhou Xiaoan were appointed to review and research the matter, and then report it to the association for review. (8) Xu Zuoliang proposed that the court should exercise its powers to enforce the provisional execution of judgments in cases where illegal procedures are stopped, in accordance with the latter part of Article 439, Section 2 of the Civil Procedure Law. Resolved: Forwarded to the Judicial Administration Department. (9) Xu Zuoliang proposed that when a party or its representative has appointed a lawyer as its agent, all documents should be served on the agent to facilitate the proceedings. Resolved: Forwarded to the Judicial Administration Department, requesting that all courts be notified to pay attention to the provisions of Article 133, Section 1 of the Civil Procedure Law. (10) Member Ge Jieshen reported that he also serves as the manager of the Huashang Yizhong Auction House, which does not hinder his legal work, and requested permission. Resolved: Permission granted. (11) Jiangsu High Court Detention Center, Second Prison, and Second Special Zone Prison separately stated in letters that the prisons are overcrowded and lack clothing and bedding, and requested donations. Resolved: Notify all members to donate enthusiastically, and the funds will be transferred by the association. The deadline is two weeks. The City's Two Grain Associations Submit to the Yuan and Ministry Not to Approve Exemption from Import Tax on Foreign Rice; Completion of the Yuehan Road Greatly Facilitates the Transportation of Grain to Lingnan; Good Harvests in Various Places This Year are Suitable for Circulation and Regulation 111

The Shanghai Soybean Rice Industry and Miscellaneous Grain Oil Cake Industry Associations believe that the reports that Guangdong Province has again telegraphed the central government to exempt import taxes on foreign rice, if approved, will not only leak out rights and interests, but also put farmers in the producing areas in a desperate situation. Therefore, yesterday they sent separate telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Industry, requesting that they not approve the exemption in order to reassure the people. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Nanjing sent to President Jiang of the Executive Yuan and Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industry: I recently read in the newspaper the resolution of the Executive Yuan regarding the request of various provinces and cities to prohibit the export of food, stating that food should be allowed to circulate freely within the country in order to balance supply and demand and gradually reach equilibrium. The measures proposed by various provinces and cities to restrict the export of food are not in line with economic principles or the central government's purpose of coordinating food management and are not approved. I have seen the government's intention to regulate food and protect the countryside. Recently, I heard that Guangdong Province has again proposed to exempt taxes on foreign rice, which has caused great confusion. The taxation of foreign rice started in the winter of 1933, but Guangdong Province was only able to unify the collection of taxes this year. Although Guangdong Province is a rice-deficient area, since the completion of the Yuehan Railway, rice and grain from various provinces in the Yangtze River Basin have been transported directly to Lingnan by rail and rail, which is very convenient. Rather than relying on foreign rice, it is better to obtain resources from the mainland. Moreover, there have been good harvests in various places this year, and the long-depleted rural economy has gradually shown signs of recovery. It is expected that the provinces and cities will ban the export of rice, causing rice shortages in the rice-deficient areas, high rice prices that harm the people, and low grain prices that harm farmers in the rice-producing areas. Fortunately, the central government does not approve this, allowing free circulation and balancing supply and demand. However, Guangdong Province wants to exempt taxes on foreign rice, which will not only leak out rights and interests, causing great concern, but also cause farmers in the producing areas to face obstacles to sales and fall into a desperate situation. With such obstacles, how can the rural economy be restored? Furthermore, it is not in line with economic principles or the central government's purpose of coordinating food management. Therefore, I do not avoid the risk of offending you and telegraphed to request that the chiefs review and approve the section of Guangdong Province requesting exemption from foreign rice tax and not approve it. I am extremely grateful. Gu Xinyi, Chairman of the Shanghai Soybean Rice Industry Association and the Miscellaneous Grain Oil Cake Industry Association. Jiang.

Dr. Hu Shih's Speech Yesterday: The Changing Pacific - Japanese Aggression Against China Will Lead to World War 113

According to the Central News Agency, Dr. Hu Shih, Dean of the College of Arts of Peking University, returned from attending the Pacific Conference as a representative of China. Last night at 8 o'clock, he was hosted by the International Relations Research Association, the Pacific Society, and the Joint Association of University Faculty at the International Hotel's second-floor dining hall. At about 10 o'clock, he began to deliver a speech in English to a crowded audience. The topic was "The Evolving Pacific." Dr. Hu first stated that he wanted to express a "New Pacific" in his speech. The so-called "New Pacific" refers to the evolution of the balance of power in the Pacific since 1931 and a comparison with the situation of Japan's supreme power from 1914 to 1931. The general perception is that Japan still enjoys supreme power in the Far East. This view is actually wrong. Seventeen years ago, from the outbreak of the European War until the Manchurian Incident in 1931, Japan did indeed enjoy supreme power in the Far East. During the European War, the overall situation in the Far East was entirely in the hands of Japan. Japan took the opportunity to drive out German forces from the Chinese coast and the Pacific. By 1921, the Washington Conference produced the so-called Washington Treaty, but Japan's position in the Western Hemisphere remained largely unchanged. It was not until 1931, when Japan abused its power in the Western Pacific, that its power began to decline. Dr. Hu continued, stating that China's unification was actually promoted by Japanese aggression. Japan's unlimited aggression against China may lead to a world war, and all countries in the Pacific will be drawn into the vortex. Although the countries of the Pacific love peace, the aggressive warlords will inevitably drive them into war. Wise politicians may be able to discern the evolution of the balance of power and make peaceful adjustments, that is, establish a Pacific regional peace mechanism based on the new balance of power. The United States, the Soviet Union, the United Kingdom, Japan, and China can all participate, seeking ways to adjust difficult issues to maintain the collective security of the entire Pacific. If not, the outbreak of a world war will be inevitable, and the terror of that war will be beyond our imagination.

Three Workers Injured During Demolition of Old House 115

Lu Fuji Construction Factory at 304 Xietu Road in the Nanshi area was recently contracted to build a house for the Ju family at the Yanjiabiao site on Peidong Ditch Road. At around 10:00 AM yesterday, the factory called together more than ten workers to dismantle the old house. Expansion of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Inspectorate - Promotion of Wang Dasui to Director 116

Since Director Cai Jingjun took office at the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, he has made many rectifications to Shanghai's police administration, achieving remarkable results. Recently, Director Cai reported to the Municipal Government that the Bureau's original Inspectorate only had one chief inspector and one deputy chief inspector, and that the inspectors of the various sub-bureaus and teams were working hard day and night, leading to intense work. He requested and received approval from the Municipal Government to expand the organization of the Inspectorate, which will now have one director and three chief inspectors, divided into eight sections to handle affairs. The candidate for director is Wang Dasui, the original chief inspector, and Dong Guangfu, Wang Weiming, and Ruan Yongqi have been transferred and appointed as chief inspectors of the eight sections. The list of directors for each section, it is reported, has already been internally determined and will be announced soon. The aforementioned expanded organization was implemented on the 3rd. The brief biographies of the individuals are as follows: Wang Dasui is a graduate of Tsinghua School in Beijing and holds a master's degree from the University of Michigan in the United States. He served as the chief of the Secretariat Section of the Capital Police Department. In 1929, he was appointed as a Chinese delegate to the Fifth International Police Conference in Paris and inspected the police administration of various European countries. After returning to China in 1930, he served as the principal of the Jiangsu Provincial Police Academy, a member of the Police Administration Specialist Committee of the Ministry of Interior, a member of the First Higher Examination Committee, and the director of the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital of Gansu Province. Dong Guangfu holds a master's degree in law from the National University of Toulouse in France. Wang Weiming is a graduate of the 18th class of the Japanese Army Academy. Two Silk Factories in Zhabei Shut Down - Wage Arrears Dispute Resolved - Factories Issue Two and a Half Months' Pay 117

The Yuanyuan and Yuanji silk reeling factories on Hutai Road in Zhabei were unable to operate due to a lack of raw materials and announced their closure on October 29. However, the salaries of the employees of the two factories had not been paid, causing an outcry from the workers, who petitioned the Party and government agencies and were repeatedly summoned for mediation by the Bureau of Social Affairs, but without result. Now, the Sixth District Silk Reeling Union sent personnel to negotiate with the factories. The factories sent representatives Zhou Jinbao and Sun Yongyuan to directly negotiate with the local authorities. As a result, the factories agreed to issue two and a half months' pay to all employees at their original salaries. The workers expressed their agreement, and a written record of the settlement was signed, announcing the resolution. Both labor and management presented the case to the Party and government agencies, requesting that the case be closed.

New Pharmaceutical Industry Prohibits Domestic Drugs from Impersonating Foreign Merchants 118

The National Federation of New Pharmaceutical Industry Associations yesterday issued a notice to all members nationwide stating that at the Federation's second general membership meeting, Zhou Bangjun proposed, with the joint signatures of Hu Zhaoxiang, Tu Kaizheng, Xu Xiangsun, Xu Xiaochu, Gao Peiliang, Zhu Yuquan, Xu Chao, Zhou Mengbai, and others, to prohibit domestically operated new pharmaceutical companies from impersonating foreign merchants and certain foreign goods in order to uphold the dignity of the nation. The worship of foreign goods is a great shame for our Chinese nation. Our countrymen are currently occupied with their own troubles, yet some of our colleagues in the new pharmaceutical industry are disregarding the overall situation and promoting this practice. Such a loss of conscience is deeply regrettable. The reason for this is nothing more than taking advantage of the Chinese people's mentality of worshiping imported goods to achieve their own desire for profit. Therefore, some domestically operated new pharmaceutical companies hang up foreign company signs, setting a precedent for a strange phenomenon unheard of in other countries, and causing the nation's dignity to be swept away. In order to safeguard the dignity of the nation, to eradicate the evil roots of the nation, and to enhance the character and status of our colleagues in the new pharmaceutical industry, it is necessary to strictly prohibit this practice. Therefore, the general meeting resolved in principle to pass the notice and inform all members to pay close attention and record it.

Cai Xiahu's Children Sue for Division of Property After His Death 120

Cai Xiahu, a native of Chuansha, came from a poor background and worked hard to build his business. He opened the Huishi Deng Milk Company on Xin Dagulu Road for more than ten years and accumulated assets worth hundreds of thousands of yuan. He had a son, Cai Qiuquan, who is now 38 years old, and a daughter, Cai Xiuzhen, who has married into the Li family. Qiuquan is also married to Sun Xiulin, and their children were born to Cai's first wife. Cai's second wife, Ms. Yang, is currently 46 years old. Cai enjoyed both wealth and happiness, and was expecting to enjoy a happy old age, but fate had it that he only had the ability to create wealth but not to enjoy it. He fell ill and died, leaving behind a legacy of poison, leading to litigation after his death. All of his assets were controlled by his stepmother, Ms. Yang, and his wife, Sun Xiulin, who lived a life of leisure, better than immortals. Cai Qiuquan, on the other hand, wandered around and was in dire straits. Unable to afford to sue on his own, he joined his sister, Li Cai Xiuzhen, in hiring two lawyers, Xi Mengqi and Jiang Yiping, to file a petition with the local court for the division of the estate, stating that the assets currently identified amount to 280,000 yuan, and that there are many more assets that have not yet been identified, and will be reported later. All the assets in this case should be divided into three shares for the mother and children, etc. Yesterday morning, Judge Tang held a hearing. The defendant hired lawyer Chen Tingrui, who stated in court that his client did not object to the division of the estate into three shares, but that it was necessary to review whether the asset list submitted by the plaintiff matched the assets held by the defendant. At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer immediately stated that if the submitted asset list did not match the defendant's, then it would be best for the defendant to hand over all the assets left by Cai Xiahu for division, and also to submit the will for reference. The judge then instructed both parties that since there was no dispute over the division of assets, the issue of the total amount was easy to resolve and they should attempt to settle out of court before further review, and then adjourned the court.

Continued Hearing of the Ye Qinghua Wife and Concubine Lawsuit - Awaiting Subpoena for Further Hearing 121

Ye Qinghua, 38 years old this year, is the younger brother of Ye Qinghe, a notorious international drug trafficker who is currently on the run. Ye was a teacher at Xiamen Jimei School when he met Wu Yu, a woman from his hometown. Later, Wu came to Shanghai to study at the Tongde Obstetrics School, and Ye was also in Shanghai. They fell in love as teacher and student and began living together, and have since had two daughters. Recently, Ye abandoned Wu, and Wu filed a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, accusing Ye Qinghua of seduction, obstructing public morals, and abandoning his mother and daughters. Based on the complaint, the court issued a warrant ordering Wu to escort the bailiff to summon Ye, but they did not find him. Ye's wife and her friend Chen Rong went to the Dacheng Apartment and beat Wu, causing her injuries. Wu filed a complaint with the court requesting an examination of her injuries and accused Ye's wife, Yang Zhuxia (also known as Lai Xiang), and Chen Rong of assault. Judge Sun Pengxian of the Second Special Court has already held a hearing, summoning both parties to court and consolidating the two cases for trial. The hearing was adjourned pending the summoning of witnesses. Yesterday, the case was reconvened for a continued hearing. Both parties arrived in court with their lawyers, but the second defendant in the assault case, Chen Rong, did not appear. After a brief hearing of both parties, the witness Xu Wangaiyu was summoned, who testified, "I live in the Dacheng Apartment, and Wu Yu also lives there, so I know her. That day, she (referring to Yang Zhuxia) came to my room with a woman (presumably Chen Rong). Wu happened to be in my room. I saw them and invited them in, poured tea, and asked them to sit down. They did not say a word and immediately beat Wu. People persuaded them to stop, and Wu escaped through the back door. They chased her to the street and beat her. The tea room guests in the apartment all witnessed it." At this point, the court stated that since the witness Xi Jinping and the defendant Chen Rong had not arrived, the hearing was adjourned until the afternoon of the 12th for further summons of witnesses and ordered the plaintiff to summon Chen Rong to court for further questioning.

Shanghai Pushan Villa, November of the 25th year [of the Republic], within the northern and southern Chinese-administered areas of the International Settlement, collected and buried coffins of various sizes, as follows: From the Public Concession's police departments and health departments, based on official correspondence, abandoned infant corpses within the concession, and unclaimed bodies from the Coroner's Office and various hospitals, 69 large coffins and 839 small coffins were collected. From our villa itself, 26 large coffins and 1,574 small coffins were collected. From the Nanshi Sanguantang Xieqiao branch villa and various charitable halls in the French Concession, 360 small coffins were collected. From the First Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross Society on Haig Road, 1 large coffin was collected. From Tongren Hospital, 2 large coffins were collected. From Renji Hospital, 1 large coffin was collected. From the Chinese Women's Relief Association's orphanage, 2 large coffins were collected. From Lianyi Charitable Association, 3 large coffins and 14 small coffins were collected. From Da Zhonghua Sanatorium, 1 small coffin was collected. From Tongde Hospital, 1 small coffin was collected. From Cihang Hospital, 1 small coffin was collected. From Hongkou Maternity Hospital, 1 small coffin was collected. In total, 104 large coffins and 2,796 small coffins were collected. A total of 1,208 coffins of various sizes were distributed. All the above corpses were collected and transported by the villa's vehicles to the charity burial ground at Dachang Tangqiao for burial, with markers erected for future identification and claim. Haizhou Salt Still Difficult to Transport to Hankou; Zhonghe Ship Aground 131

Since the water level of the Yangtze River has fallen sharply, the Haizhou salt that is shipped to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has been blocked. Some Haizhou ships in the upper reaches have been stranded for months, and they have only recently been able to unload. Although the freight cost of transporting salt has increased by one time, the shipping companies still dare not risk taking on the shipments, fearing that they will be stranded midway and unable to load or unload, resulting in huge losses, which would be a real loss. Therefore, for the past month, the amount of Haizhou salt accumulated for shipment has increased daily, and the salt merchants are anxious to ship it. Recently, due to the gradual increase in the water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, to two feet and four inches, the river ships can pass to and fro. The salt merchants are planning to transport Chen Jia.

Chen Bingrong from Jiaxing, the accountant of Qiming Dyeing and Weaving Factory at No. 260 Edward Road, who is 24 years old, recently colluded with brokers Xu Yixiang (22 years old) from Songjiang, apprentice Huang Bozheng (20 years old) from Ningbo, and Wu Hongda (21 years old) from Wenzhou, and others, and used public funds from the factory to engage in yarn and flower speculation. They also frequented prostitutes and gambled, and contracted venereal diseases. Recently, the price of yarn and flowers has fluctuated greatly, so Chen and others have lost tens of thousands of yuan. On the 1st of this month, the manager, Zhu Wen, suddenly investigated the accounts and immediately discovered that there was a shortage of 5,000 yuan. After detailed investigation, it was found that it was not 5,000 yuan, but more than 40,000 yuan, so he investigated it. Chen confessed that it was caused by the failure of speculation with Wu Yixiang and others. Fearing that the manager would sue the officials, he secretly swallowed a bottle of potion and committed suicide. After being discovered, he was immediately sent to the hospital for treatment. Because he was determined to die, he could not be saved and died at 4:00 pm. The hospital telegraphed the General Patrol Room, and the Chinese detectives Zhang Mingde, Jiang Shangpei, and Bao Tan Zhou Zhenxing rushed to the scene and took Chen to the Fielun Road Coroner's Office. On the 2nd, the prosecutor of the First Special Court verified the body, ordered it to be coffined and buried. The detectives then found out this embezzlement case, so they went to the Qiming Factory the day before yesterday and arrested the three people, Xu, Huang, and Wu. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The patrol room lawyer Ru Baoyi stated the previous situation, because the accounts were numerous and the investigation was time-consuming, so he requested permission to be detained for investigation. He also said that the current defendants' guarantee deposit in the exchange reached more than 10,000 yuan, and the patrol room has been notified to seize it, etc. Judge Feng Shide reviewed and reported it, and then ordered Xu and others to be detained for one week for further interrogation. The salt was loaded on the pier, and the Zhonghe ship (2,030 tons) of the Shanghai Huatong Shipping Company, with a draft of 18 feet, was rented to load salt. Yesterday, it opened to Chenjiagang and sailed into the Twelve Forts port. The highest tide there is only 13 feet, so the Zhonghe ship was immediately stranded in the port and could not move. Yesterday, the shipowner telegraphed Shanghai to report. A ship has now been sent to tow it for rescue. In fact, it is still impossible to ship Haizhou salt to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River.

Workers of Yizhong Electric Porcelain East Factory Petition, Presenting Five Demands 133

The workers of the west factory of Yizhong Electric Porcelain Factory went on strike. After mediation by the Social Bureau, the preconditions were agreed upon and the matter was temporarily resolved. More than 350 workers from the east factory of Yizhong Fuji Porcelain Electric Company in Lingjiaqiao, Yangjing Town, Pudong, also changed their treatment rules by the factory. All the preferential treatment methods in the past were cancelled. The labor union has repeatedly asked the factory to maintain the original treatment, but without result. The workers are panicked because they cannot maintain their livelihoods. Yesterday, they specially sent representatives Zhang Heshang, Gao Julin, Zhang Yougui, and more than a dozen others to the Fenglinqiao Municipal Party Headquarters to petition. Lu Yinchu, a cadre of the Civil Movement Section, received them. After the workers put forward five conditions, (1) Those who earn less than 10 yuan in wages should increase by 20%, and those who earn more than 10 yuan should increase by 10%. (2) If they are laid off, they should be rewarded with wages if they work continuously for one month after the start of work. (3) Regardless of whether they are male or female workers, if they work on Sundays or night shifts, they should be based on the standard of day workers. A All Class A work. (4) Wages should be increased once a year as usual. (5) Workers must not be dismissed without reason. Lu said that he accepted and would handle it together with the Social Bureau.

However, her husband had married three wives, and he said that a wife was a dish that he wanted to change the taste of, so he framed her, meaning that he was tired of eating small dishes and wanted to change the taste, so she asked for justice. At this point, Ma Sunxi testified that the plaintiff lived in Dongcun, and he lived in Xicun. They did not communicate, nor did he commit adultery with Gu. Opening a room in the Sutai Hotel was because he and his wife went to his uncle's house, so he stayed with his wife in the clan hall. How could he call a stag a horse? His relationship with his wife was very good, and she was illiterate, so how could she write a letter? His wife could testify to this. At this point, Ma Sunshi was summoned and testified that she was 34 years old, and Ma Sunxi was her husband. Their relationship was very good. She had never written a letter. Xi Daosheng wrote it in her name. Mr. Gao saw him write it. As for going to the Sutai Hotel, she stayed with her husband, etc. After the court verified the confession, the case was found to be bizarre and ordered to be investigated, and Xi Daosheng was summoned to court for questioning, and then the court adjourned.

An order was issued to all Chinese and Western detectives under their command to tighten the search for the murderers. Under the investigation of Inspector Jin Jiulin, Detectives Zhou Buguang, Zhou Bingcheng, Lin Yilong, and Li Jinzhang, the murderer of the Yin case was finally found. It turned out that the husband of a woman from Anhui, Sun Er Guniang (38 years old this year, residing at No. 8 Chongfu Lane, Route Foch), was arrested and imprisoned by Yin Bengen for theft. Yin then had an affair with Sun Er Guniang. However, Sun Er Guniang became fickle and in recent months became acquainted with Wang Dianhua (also known as Lao Wu, 34 years old), a fellow villager residing at No. 1, Lane 984, Route Petain in the French Concession, leading to Wang and Yin becoming enemies due to jealousy. Moreover, Wang had a friend who was also a thief and was arrested and imprisoned after being reported by a detective. Therefore, Wang hated Yin deeply and planned to have Yin killed to eliminate the harm and vent his anger. Inspector Jin obtained this lead and learned that Wang Dianhua's wife had recently died of illness and the funeral was scheduled for the afternoon of the 2nd. He led the detectives Tao Rongling, Wu Wengang, etc., to the address around 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd and arrested Wang Yi Gong Dai Dianhua, Wu Weicai, Sun Er Guniang, Liang Yuguang, Zhao Shilai, Zhong Jizhuo, Ji Yegen, Zhang Chengzhi, Wu Huari, Yang Yuanshu, Liang Houyu, and other eleven men and women. They were taken to the police station. Wang confessed to killing Yin, but the handgun used for the murder could not be retrieved. At noon yesterday, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. Attorney Gu Shouxi of the Police Department explained the case and requested a two-week adjournment to investigate the details of the case before filing for trial. Detective Tao Ronglin then reported the process of arresting the defendants. When Wang Dianhua was interrogated, he confessed that he, Wang Kaifu, who was at large, and Ma Changshou killed Yin. Because Yin had an affair with Wang Kaifu's sister, Wang Kaifu called me to go. We took two handguns and fired five shots. I was on the side and did not hold a handgun. Wu Weicai confessed that he did not go at the time but knew about the killing of Yin Bengen afterwards. Sun Er Guniang confessed that she had an affair with Yin Bengen and did not know Wang Dianhua. The other eight defendants claimed that they went to carry the coffin or attended the funeral of Wang Dianhua's wife and were arrested without knowing anything about the murder. Wang Dianhua also confessed that the handgun belonged to Ma Changshou. Witness Shao Wangshi testified that the deceased (Bengen) ran into my living room that night, and he (referring to Wang Dianhua) chased in with a handgun and told the deceased to come out. The deceased was stubborn, and I told them to go out. He (referring to Wang) scared me with a handgun and forbade me to make a sound. Then a short man dragged the deceased out and shot him to death. Yin Bengen's wife and daughter also came to the court and requested a strict investigation to seek justice. After verification of the confessions by Judge Wang Gangxu, the hearing was adjourned to the 19th, and the defendants were remanded in custody. The investigating detectives were instructed to report to the court for the release of any defendants found to be unrelated to the case.

Overview of Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Changes in September of the 25th Year 150

— Compiled by the China Credit Information Service

(Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview, No. 39)

The state of industry and commerce in Shanghai this month outwardly exhibits a striking appearance of prosperity. The 52 newly established firms are the highest monthly record this year. Closures were only one more than the previous month, maintaining the downward trend since June. However, a closer look reveals that this abnormal prosperity is due to the recent emergence of a large number of so-called "escort agencies." The continued sluggishness of the manufacturing industry and the gradual decline of the retail sector remain significant obstacles to the city's prosperity. Nevertheless, compared with the same period last year, the actual number of industrial and commercial households in Shanghai this year is much better than last year. A total of 52 new establishments, 13 expansions, 3 contractions, 210 reorganizations, and 59 closures were recorded this month. Compared to the past two months and the same period last year, the figures are as follows:

New Establishment Expansion Contraction Reorganization Closure

July, 25th Year 34 20 22 130 71

August 27 16 9 235 58

September 52 13 3 210 59

September, 24th Year 25 — — 221 84

The number of new establishments this month increased by 25 compared to the previous month and 27 compared to the same period last year. Expansions decreased by 3 compared to the previous month. Contractions decreased by 6 compared to the previous month. Reorganizations decreased by 25 compared to the previous month and 11 compared to the same period last year. Closures increased by 1 compared to the previous month and decreased by 25 compared to the same period last year. The distribution of these figures among various industries this month is as follows:

New Establishment Expansion Contraction Reorganization Closure

Special Industries 29 5 1 67 13

Manufacturing Industry 7 2 1 33 10

Retail Commerce 16 6 1 110 36

Total 52 13 3 210 59

The number of new establishments in the special industries category increased by 20 compared to the previous month, and closures decreased by 18 compared to the previous month, a rare phenomenon. The reason is the successive appearance of escort agencies, as mentioned earlier. Due to the sluggish market and the depression in various industries, the former "escort houses" have mostly transformed into dance halls for those with greater financial resources, while those with weaker funds have changed their names and identities, all calling themselves "escorts." The financial industry in the special industries category was relatively quiet this month. The more important changes in other industries include the following:

(1) The Six Nations Hotel Ceases Operation and Liquidates. This hotel was originally formed from the reorganization of the former Quan Jia Fu Western Restaurant and the Continental Hotel. It only opened for business in July of this year. Manager Gu Yuanlong and Assistant Manager Li Yongqing were appointed. At the time of opening, the business was affected by the sluggish market and was not prosperous. Eventually, internal staff carried out dishonest acts, and shareholders had differing opinions. Assistant Manager Li even took all the account books, vouchers, and cash and left, making it impossible to operate. The hotel was forced to announce the cessation of business and liquidation.

(2) Jinlan Xieji Food Company's Liquidation Call. This company was formerly known as the Jinlan Hotel Food Company, which was quite large in scale and could be called one of the giants in the Cantonese industry. It has been in business for more than two years since its opening. Initially, the business was booming and its reputation was growing. However, due to the recent decline in the market, the business plummeted. It was later transferred and reorganized into the Jinlan Xieji Food Company at the end of March of this year, but the market remained sluggish, and the business did not improve. As a result, the loss was significant. It was extended to the 10th of this month, and finally, due to the inability to maintain operations, the liquidation call was announced. It is said that the debts owed can be offset against each other. (To be continued)

Finally, the score reached 34 to 31 with 45 seconds remaining. The Hornets planned to take a long shot to try to win, but inadvertently neglected their defense, allowing Han Zhenyuan to score a goal. Education News

Cultural Circles Support the Suiyuan Movement 171

Municipal Education Association In order to promote the one-day sports of the education associations in various districts to achieve good results, the Shanghai Municipal Education Association held a joint meeting of the heads of various districts at the association yesterday (3rd) afternoon at 3:00 PM. The permanent heads of the districts were present: Tao Guangchuan of District 1, Wang Dingcheng of District 2, Xu Peiheng of District 3, Tong Zhifu of the West District, Shen Banmei of District 5, Xi Feiyuan of District 6, Diao Qingen of District 7, Jin Kehao of District 8, Wu Rugui of District 9, Hou Junren of District 10, and Jiang Ce of District 11. The meeting was chaired by Huang Zaoxiong, the standing director of the association. The following items were agreed upon: (1) The education associations in various districts under the association should actively carry out the one-day sports together with the principals of various schools; (2) The association has stipulated that the education associations in various districts of supplementary schools should promote amateur learning for citizens and should start to do so immediately; (3) The councils of the education associations in various districts should hold more meetings to promote association affairs.

Zhonghua Vocational School The Nanshi Lujiabang Zhonghua Vocational School held a Suiyuan support movement some time ago due to the invasion of bandits and puppets. In addition to remitting the 400 yuan raised to the front, they continued their efforts. Teachers and students donated money on a monthly basis. Once a certain amount has been collected, it will be remitted again. Yesterday, they also held a general mobilization to solicit gloves and silk cotton vests. On the one hand, they also solicited donations from familiar stores, raising about 200 vests and 4,000 pairs of gloves, which were limited to being prepared by the 12th of this month. There were also many other national currency items. Although there were only forty or fifty girls in the school, under the guidance of female teachers, they were working day and night to make them.

Peiming Girls' Middle School The teachers and students of Peiming Girls' Middle School on Hedde Road in this port donated a total of more than 1,200 yuan through donations and salary donations. Yesterday, they purchased all the clothing materials, and the students were sewing them, which can be completed and sent to Suiyuan within three days.

Municipal Zhongshan Elementary School Shanghai Municipal Zhongshan Elementary School held a fundraising campaign. The students donated 13.39 yuan in silver, and 15 copper coins were sent to Shen Bao to be remitted to the front to express their condolences.

The Ministry of Education's Medical Education Committee Investigates National Medical Schools 172

The Ministry of Education's Medical Education Committee, according to the resolution of the last National Medical School Presidents' Conference, investigated the general situation of national medical schools. Annual reports must be prepared at the end of the year for verification. The committee has prepared 21 kinds of annual report investigation forms for medical colleges and medical, pharmaceutical, and dental specialized schools, including the affiliated staff, nurses, doctors, academic conferences, and the history, organization, assets, funds, equipment, construction, health, inspection of each school, as well as the number of students, graduates, curriculum allocation, newly added books, specimens, instruments, etc., and the actual situation of teaching. On the 2nd, a general letter was sent by the conference to all medical colleges and schools in the country, limiting the time for filling in the report within one month.

The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund Recruits Students to Study in the UK at Public Expense, Covering 21 Fields Such as Astronomy and Physics 173

Starting on February 1st next year, the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund Management Committee will begin recruiting the fifth batch of students to study in the UK at public expense. The number of places is 29, and the distribution of academic fields is as follows: 2 in astronomy, one focusing on mathematical astronomy and one focusing on physical astronomy, open to graduates of astronomy, mathematics, and physics departments; 1 in physics, focusing on theoretical physics, open to graduates of physics or mathematics departments; 1 in chemistry, focusing on physical chemistry, open to graduates of chemistry or physics departments; 2 in geography, focusing on natural geography and cartography, open to graduates of geography, geology, and geomatics departments; 1 in agricultural chemistry, focusing on soil fertility, open to graduates of agricultural chemistry and agronomy departments; 1 in plant pathology, open to graduates of plant and horticulture departments; 1 in animal husbandry, open to graduates of animal husbandry, veterinary medicine, animal, and biology departments; 2 in veterinary medicine, open to graduates of veterinary specialized schools or agricultural colleges and medical schools; 1 in fisheries, focusing on marine fisheries, open to graduates of fisheries specialized schools or science colleges and animal and biology departments; 1 in mechanical engineering, open to graduates of mechanical or electrical engineering departments; 1 in hydraulic engineering, open to graduates of hydraulic specialized schools or civil engineering departments of engineering colleges; 1 in aeronautical engineering, open to graduates of mechanical engineering, physics, and mathematics departments; open to graduates of textile chemical engineering departments; 1 in sanitary engineering, open to graduates of sanitary engineering, civil engineering, or hydraulic engineering departments; 2 in theoretical medicine, one focusing on pathology and one focusing on pharmacology, open to graduates of medical schools; 1 in general linguistics, open to graduates of linguistics or literature departments; 1 in social anthropology, open to graduates of history or sociology departments; 1 in finance, focusing on taxation, open to graduates of business schools or economics departments of law schools; 1 in railway management, open to graduates of railway management schools or civil engineering departments; 1 in statistics, open to graduates of business schools, economics departments of law schools, sociology departments of liberal arts colleges, or mathematics departments of science colleges; 1 in social legislation, open to graduates of sociology departments of liberal arts colleges, economics departments of law schools, or business administration departments of business schools. In addition to applying for the exam with the qualifications of a major, applicants can also apply for the exam with the subjects they have studied in the minor, but they must have a school certificate. The application date is from February 1st to March 10th, 26, and late applications will not be accepted. The exam dates and locations are from April 1st to 6th, 26, held simultaneously in Nanjing and Beiping. Those who are interested in taking the exam can request an application form from the office of the association on Shanxi Road, Nanjing.

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Investigates School-Age Children in the City from the 11th to the 30th of This Month 175

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau announced, "Investigating the promotion of compulsory education is an important plan for the restoration of China, and investigating school-age children is the foundation for promoting compulsory education. The city has a dense population and many school-age children. In order to understand the situation of school-age children and facilitate the promotion of compulsory education, the bureau has decided to investigate school-age children in the city from December 11th to 31st of this year, assigning municipal and some private school teachers and high-grade students to be responsible for the investigation. The investigators will all wear investigation certificates for identification. This announcement is hereby made to the residents of the city, so that they are aware of this matter. When encountering investigators, they should report truthfully and should not be suspicious. This order."

The Registration of Scout Servicemen in the City Will Close Today; Late Registration Will Not Allow Election; Wartime Service Corps Is Actively Organizing 177

The Shanghai Scout Council, in preparation for the election of the fifth council, has submitted it to the General Assembly for record and began to re-register servicemen in the city on the 22nd of last month. It is known that the association is scheduled to close at 6:00 PM today, and late registration will not be allowed. Therefore, today is the last opportunity for servicemen in the city to register, otherwise they will lose the right to vote and be elected. It is also known that hundreds of people have registered with the association in recent days. Once the registration procedures are completed, the date will be announced, and the next council will be re-elected. It is also known that the detailed measures of the Scout Wartime Service Corps have been drafted and will be announced and implemented as soon as the council meeting passes it, and actively organize it to be established as soon as possible.

Hu Shih Expresses Grief Over the Closure of "Independent Critic," General Public Pays Close Attention, Mr. Hu Will Postpone His Return to Beiping 179

Hu Shih's "Independent Critic" was suddenly ordered to cease publication late on the second day by the Hebei-Chahar authorities. According to Mr. Hu, he only learned of this after reading the newspaper and does not yet know the details. He will telegraph to Beiping to inquire about the specifics. Mr. Hu expressed deep sorrow and said he would not be able to go north today. His scheduled speech at the YMCA on the afternoon of the third has been canceled. It is difficult to find a suitable venue in Shanghai for the time being, so he will no longer give speeches here. Since its publication, "Independent Critic" has had many readers among the intellectual class because its writers include Mr. Hu himself, as well as Weng Wenhao, Jiang Tingfu, Ren Shuyong, Chen Hengzhe, Xian Yuxiu, Pan Guangdan, Zhou Binglin, and others who are all highly respected figures of their time. The reason for the forced closure is reportedly due to two articles: one written by Binglin on the 8th, and the other by Zhang Xiruo on the 229th. Both articles were allegedly feared by certain parties, leading to the order to cease publication. Currently, the general public here is paying close attention to this matter.

Yarn and Cotton Prices Surge Twenty Yuan in Three Days, Yarn Prices Slightly Rebound Yesterday, Near-Term Three to Four Yuan, Long-Term Estimated at Five Yuan, High Prices Still Seen at Two Hundred Sixty-Two Yuan 180

The yarn market has been soaring continuously, prompting profit-taking and a sudden reaction. There is also a shortage of spot yarn, so some parties with large holdings are not letting go. The momentum is still tired but perky. However, after rising about twenty yuan in the last three days, the market price has stabilized somewhat, and bulls are releasing large quantities, causing market sentiment to decline. This kind of reversal is also expected. In the afternoon, it was rumored that EWO offered 500 bales of 20s Five Rams and Shepherd yarns at a price of 250 yuan including tax.

The Market Began to Decline in the Afternoon

The forward market opened with December contracts rising sharply due to reports of severe labor unrest in Qingdao, causing people to expect higher prices. Retail investors covered their short positions, and the bullish trend intensified, with the peak reaching 260 yuan. When trading in long-term contracts, the momentum was slightly calmer. In the second session, the market retreated due to weak raw cotton prices and large-scale selling by major players. At the same time, the rise in Osaka Sanpin yarn was not strong, and the momentum was weak. As a result, the closing price for this month was 1.4 yuan higher than the previous day, while long-term contracts fell by 1 to 1.5 yuan. When the market opened in the afternoon, major players sold off, and the Sanpin yarn market also declined, loosening the market. All months fell by 1.9 to 2.4 yuan. The second session rose slightly. By the third closing, rumors circulated that EWO had offered 2,000 bales, leading to increased selling. As a result, all months plummeted by 3.9 to 4.7 yuan from the morning closing price. Three Major Reasons for the Surge in the Yarn Market, Reaching a New High Since the Eighth Year of the Republic, The Margin for This Month's Futures Increased to Thirty-Four Yuan 182

The situation in the yarn and cloth market has suddenly developed rapidly. During this period, the price of December yarn rose from more than 230 yuan to 60 yuan, breaking through four major levels in succession. New peaks have emerged one after another. Yesterday, a new high price of 262 yuan was seen, which is the highest peak since the eighth year of the Republic. There are three reasons for this: First, our country has had a bumper harvest in both spring and autumn. Farmers have been in dire straits for five years, and their economies have been able to recover slightly. The market for cloth has been the first to become active. Second, yarn factories have suffered five years of adversity, and raw cotton has been expensive and yarn cheap for many years. Yarn factories have almost been in a state of bankruptcy. In addition, Chen cotton for July and August of this year was sold short, raising the price to 52.5 yuan. The yarn price was still in a state of exhaustion. At that time, the price of near-term futures yarn was 193.1 yuan, and factories were losing money. Some yarn factories were under financial pressure and unable to turn around, so they announced shutdowns and reduced production, resulting in a sharp decrease in production volume and dwindling inventories. Several factories in North China have been purchased by Japanese merchants, which shows the severity of the difficulties faced by yarn factories. Later, in the autumn, because the weather was favorable, with timely rain, cotton and rice had a bumper harvest across the country. Buyers from the south and the upper reaches of the Yangtze River flocked to purchase, so the factories had no large quantities of spot yarn to supply. First, they purchased 30,000 bales of yarn from their warehouses, and then they expected the price of futures yarn to rise. Third, because the trend of government bond margins was bleak, general speculators changed direction and shifted their focus, flocking to the cotton and yarn market. As a result, the number of trading chips increased sharply. The trading volume for the four-month period has accumulated to a huge 1,054,150 bales. As trading increased, the fluctuations became even greater. The market closes late every day. General speculators are following the trend, and the rises and falls are difficult to predict. In order to avoid danger, the exchange authorities have increased the special margin for December futures yarn by three batches, totaling 24 yuan. Including the original margin of 10 yuan per bale, the total is 34 yuan. The remaining months have been increased by two batches per bale, totaling 16 yuan. Including the original margin of 10 yuan, the total is 26 yuan. The current price of 20s Jincheng yarn, including tax, has reached 276 yuan, and 42s Jincheng has reached 405 yuan. In fact, the yarn industry has been in decline for five years, and it seems that the good times are coming.

American Cotton Sentiment is Extremely Excited, Short Selling is Gradually Decreasing, Spot Goods are Strong 183

Yesterday, when the American cotton market opened, the prices of all months fell by 2 points, but rose by 4 points. In the early morning, traders bought December contracts. The Liverpool market was active, and new customers from outside the industry were buying, causing prices to rise firmly. Sentiment is very excited because short selling is gradually decreasing and spot goods are strong, and the prices of all goods are rising. Then, due to profit-taking by bulls, there was a partial reaction. There was considerable discussion about the government's sale of loan cotton, but there was no official announcement from the government. The market closed firm. Spot goods rose by 5 points, futures rose by 5 to 9 points, English cotton spot goods rose by 5 points, and futures rose by 96 points. Indian cotton initially rose due to purchases by Japanese merchants, but then fell back due to the decline in Japanese yarn and the rush of cotton farmers to sell. In the end, it rose again due to the strength of the stock market and short covering. Pingguoer rose by 1 to 1.25 rupees, Aomula rose by 2 rupees, and Bairoxi rose by 1.5 rupees.
